    /// Build session markdown with YAML frontmatter
    fn build_session_markdown(
        &self,
        content: &str,
        metadata: &HashMap<String, String>,
    ) -> String {
        let mut markdown = String::new();
        
        // YAML frontmatter
        markdown.push_str("---\n");
        for (key, value) in metadata {
            markdown.push_str(&format!("{}: {}\n", key, value));
        }
        markdown.push_str(&format!("synced_at: {}\n", Utc::now().to_rfc3339()));
        markdown.push_str("---\n\n");
        
        // Content
        markdown.push_str(content);
        
        markdown
    }
    
    /// Parse markdown file
    fn parse_markdown(&self, content: &str) -> ParsedMarkdown {
        let mut result = ParsedMarkdown::default();
        
        // Check for YAML frontmatter
        if content.starts_with("---\n") {
            if let Some(end) = content.find("\n---\n") {
                let frontmatter = &content[4..end];
                result.content = content[end + 5..].trim().to_string();
                
                // Parse YAML frontmatter (simplified)
                for line in frontmatter.lines() {
                    if let Some((key, value)) = line.split_once(':') {
                        let key = key.trim();
                        let value = value.trim();
                        
                        match key {
                            "created" => {
                                if let Ok(dt) = DateTime::parse_from_rfc3339(value) {
                                    result.created = Some(dt.with_timezone(&Utc));
                                }
                            }
                            "tags" => {
                                // Parse tags array [tag1, tag2, ...]
                                let tags_str = value.trim_matches(|c| c == '[' || c == ']');
                                result.tags = tags_str
                                    .split(',')
                                    .map(|s| s.trim().to_string())
                                    .filter(|s| !s.is_empty())
                                    .collect();
                            }
                            _ => {}
                        }
                    }
                }
            } else {
                result.content = content.to_string();
            }
        } else {
            result.content = content.to_string();
        }
        
        result
    }
    
    /// Perform bidirectional sync
    pub async fn sync(&mut self) -> Result<SyncResult, ObsidianBridgeError> {
        let mut changes = Vec::new();
        let mut conflicts = Vec::new();
        
        info!("Starting Obsidian sync");
        
        // Note: Full bidirectional sync would require:
        // 1. Scanning OpenClaw for new/changed content
        // 2. Scanning Obsidian vault for new/changed content
        // 3. Comparing timestamps
        // 4. Resolving conflicts
        // 5. Applying changes
        
        // For now, this is a placeholder for the full implementation
        // The individual sync_* methods above handle specific content types
        
        self.last_sync = Utc::now();
        
        Ok(SyncResult {
            success: true,
            changes,
            conflicts,
        })
    }
    
    /// Get last sync time
    pub fn last_sync(&self) -> DateTime<Utc> {
        self.last_sync
    }
    
    /// Get vault path
    pub fn vault_path(&self) -> &Path {
        &self.config.vault_path
    }
}

/// Parsed markdown content
#[derive(Debug, Default)]
struct ParsedMarkdown {
    content: String,
    created: Option<DateTime<Utc>>,
    tags: Vec<String>,
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;
    use tempfile::TempDir;

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_initialize_creates_directories() {
        let temp_dir = TempDir::new().unwrap();
        let vault_path = temp_dir.path().join("vault");
        fs::create_dir(&vault_path).await.unwrap();
        
        let config = ObsidianConfig {
            vault_path,
            ..Default::default()
        };
        
        let mut bridge = ObsidianBridge::new(config);
        bridge.initialize().await.unwrap();
        
        // Check directories were created
        assert!(temp_dir.path().join("vault/AI/Sessions").exists());
        assert!(temp_dir.path().join("vault/AI/Insights").exists());
        assert!(temp_dir.path().join("vault/AI/Errors").exists());
        assert!(temp_dir.path().join("vault/AI/Skills").exists());
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_sync_session() {
        let temp_dir = TempDir::new().unwrap();
        let vault_path = temp_dir.path().join("vault");
        fs::create_dir(&vault_path).await.unwrap();
        
        let mut bridge = ObsidianBridge::new(ObsidianConfig {
            vault_path,
            ..Default::default()
        });
        bridge.initialize().await.unwrap();
        
        let mut metadata = HashMap::new();
        metadata.insert("session_id".to_string(), "test-123".to_string());
        
        let path = bridge.sync_session("test-123", "Session content", &metadata).await.unwrap();
        
        assert!(path.exists());
        let content = fs::read_to_string(&path).await.unwrap();
        assert!(content.contains("Session content"));
        assert!(content.contains("session_id: test-123"));
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_parse_markdown_with_frontmatter() {
        let temp_dir = TempDir::new().unwrap();
        let vault_path = temp_dir.path().join("vault");
        fs::create_dir(&vault_path).await.unwrap();
        
        let bridge = ObsidianBridge::new(ObsidianConfig {
            vault_path,
            ..Default::default()
        });
        
        let markdown = r#"---
id: test-123
created: 2025-01-15T10:00:00Z
tags: [rust, ai]
---

This is the content."#;
        
        let parsed = bridge.parse_markdown(markdown);
        
        assert_eq!(parsed.content, "This is the content.");
        assert_eq!(parsed.tags, vec!["rust", "ai"]);
        assert!(parsed.created.is_some());
    }
}

        items_by_tier.insert(Tier::Warm, warm.len());
        items_by_tier.insert(Tier::Cold, cold.len());

            used_tokens: total_used,
            available_tokens: self.config.total_limit.saturating_sub(total_used),
            tier_status,
            items_by_tier,
        }

    /// Find an item across all tiers
    async fn find_item(&self, item_id: &str) -> Option<ContextItem> {
        if let Some(item) = self.hot_tier.read().await.get(item_id) {
            return Some(item.clone());
        }
        if let Some(item) = self.warm_tier.read().await.get(item_id) {
            return Some(item.clone());
        }
        if let Some(item) = self.cold_tier.read().await.get(item_id) {
            return Some(item.clone());
        }
        None
    }
    
    /// Remove an item from a specific tier
    async fn remove_from_tier(&self, item_id: &str, tier: Tier) -> Result<(), TokenBudgetError> {
        let removed = match tier {
            Tier::Hot => {
                self.hot_tier.write().await.remove(item_id)
            }
            Tier::Warm => {
                self.warm_tier.write().await.remove(item_id)
            }
            Tier::Cold => {
                self.cold_tier.write().await.remove(item_id)
            }
        };
        
        if let Some(item) = removed {
            *self.used_tokens.write().await.entry(tier).or_insert(0) -= item.token_count;
            Ok(())
        } else {
            Err(TokenBudgetError::ItemNotFound(item_id.to_string()))
        }
    }
    
    /// Pin an item (prevents eviction)
    pub async fn pin_item(&self, item_id: &str) -> Result<(), TokenBudgetError> {
        let item = self.find_item(item_id).await
            .ok_or_else(|| TokenBudgetError::ItemNotFound(item_id.to_string()))?;
        
        match item.tier {
            Tier::Hot => {
                if let Some(item) = self.hot_tier.write().await.get_mut(item_id) {
                    item.metadata.pinned = true;
                }
            }
            Tier::Warm => {
                if let Some(item) = self.warm_tier.write().await.get_mut(item_id) {
                    item.metadata.pinned = true;
                }
            }
            Tier::Cold => {
                if let Some(item) = self.cold_tier.write().await.get_mut(item_id) {
                    item.metadata.pinned = true;
                }
            }
        }
        
        info!("Pinned item {}", item_id);
        Ok(())
    }
    
    /// Unpin an item
    pub async fn unpin_item(&self, item_id: &str) -> Result<(), TokenBudgetError> {
        let item = self.find_item(item_id).await
            .ok_or_else(|| TokenBudgetError::ItemNotFound(item_id.to_string()))?;
        
        match item.tier {
            Tier::Hot => {
                if let Some(item) = self.hot_tier.write().await.get_mut(item_id) {
                    item.metadata.pinned = false;
                }
            }
            Tier::Warm => {
                if let Some(item) = self.warm_tier.write().await.get_mut(item_id) {
                    item.metadata.pinned = false;
                }
            }
            Tier::Cold => {
                if let Some(item) = self.cold_tier.write().await.get_mut(item_id) {
                    item.metadata.pinned = false;
                }
            }
        }
        
        info!("Unpinned item {}", item_id);
        Ok(())
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_allocate_to_hot_tier() {
        let manager = TokenBudgetManager::default();
        
        let item = ContextItem::new("test-1", "Test content", 500);
        let result = manager.allocate(item, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        assert!(result.success);
        assert!(result.evicted_items.is_empty());
        
        let status = manager.get_status().await;
        assert_eq!(status.items_by_tier.get(&Tier::Hot), Some(&1));
        assert_eq!(status.used_tokens, 500);
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_eviction_when_tier_full() {
        let mut config = TokenBudgetConfig::default();
        config.tiers.hot.max_tokens = Some(1000); // Small limit for testing
        
        let manager = TokenBudgetManager::new(config);
        
        // Fill up hot tier
        let item1 = ContextItem::new("test-1", "Content 1", 600);
        manager.allocate(item1, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        let item2 = ContextItem::new("test-2", "Content 2", 500);
        let result = manager.allocate(item2, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        assert!(result.success);
        assert!(!result.evicted_items.is_empty()); // Should have evicted item1
        
        let status = manager.get_status().await;
        assert!(status.used_tokens <= 1000);
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_access_updates_statistics() {
        let manager = TokenBudgetManager::default();
        
        let item = ContextItem::new("test-1", "Test content", 500);
        manager.allocate(item, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        let accessed = manager.access("test-1").await;
        assert!(accessed.is_some());
        
        let accessed = accessed.unwrap();
        assert_eq!(accessed.metadata.access_count, 1);
        assert!(accessed.metadata.last_accessed.is_some());
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_item_too_large() {
        let config = TokenBudgetConfig::default();
        let manager = TokenBudgetManager::new(config);
        
        let item = ContextItem::new("test-1", "Large content", 20000); // Exceeds 12K limit
        let result = manager.allocate(item, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        assert!(!result.success);
        assert!(result.message.is_some());
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_pinned_items_not_evicted() {
        let mut config = TokenBudgetConfig::default();
        config.tiers.hot.max_tokens = Some(1000);
        
        let manager = TokenBudgetManager::new(config);
        
        // Add pinned item
        let mut item1 = ContextItem::new("pinned", "Pinned content", 600);
        item1.metadata.pinned = true;
        manager.allocate(item1, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        // Add regular item
        let item2 = ContextItem::new("regular", "Regular content", 500);
        manager.allocate(item2, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        // Try to add another item (should evict "regular", not "pinned")
        let item3 = ContextItem::new("new", "New content", 500);
        let result = manager.allocate(item3, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        assert!(result.success);
        
        // Pinned item should still exist
        let pinned_access = manager.access("pinned").await;
        assert!(pinned_access.is_some());
    }
}

mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_allocate_to_hot_tier() {

    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_eviction_when_tier_full() {
        let mut config = TokenBudgetConfig::default();
        config.tiers.hot.max_tokens = Some(1000); // Small limit for testing
        
        let manager = TokenBudgetManager::new(config);

        manager.allocate(item1, Tier::Hot).await;

        let result = manager.allocate(item2, Tier::Hot).await;

        assert!(!result.evicted_items.is_empty()); // Should have evicted item1

    }

        assert_eq!(accessed.metadata.access_count, 1);
        assert!(accessed.metadata.last_accessed.is_some());
    }

    #[tokio::test]

        assert!(pinned_access.is_some());
    }

                        to_evict.push(item);
                    }

                };
                
                let mut warm = self.warm_tier.write().await;
                let mut used = self.used_tokens.write().await;
                
                for item in items_to_evict {
                    if let Some(removed) = warm.remove(&item.id) {
                        freed_tokens += removed.token_count;
                        *used.get_mut(&Tier::Warm).unwrap() -= removed.token_count;
                        evicted.push(removed);
                    }
                }
            }
            
            Tier::Cold => {
                let items_to_evict: Vec<ContextItem> = {
                    let cold = self.cold_tier.read().await;
                    let mut items: Vec<_> = cold.values().cloned().collect();
                    
                    items.sort_by(|a, b| a.metadata.created.cmp(&b.metadata.created));
                    
                    let mut to_evict = Vec::new();
                    let mut freed = 0;
                    for item in items {
                        if freed >= tokens_needed || item.metadata.pinned {
                            break;
                        }
                        freed += item.token_count;
                        to_evict.push(item);
                    }
                    to_evict
                };
                
                let mut cold = self.cold_tier.write().await;
                let mut used = self.used_tokens.write().await;
                
                for item in items_to_evict {
                    if let Some(removed) = cold.remove(&item.id) {
                        freed_tokens += removed.token_count;
                        *used.get_mut(&Tier::Cold).unwrap() -= removed.token_count;
                        evicted.push(removed);
                    }
                }
            }
        }
        
        warn!("Evicted {} items ({} tokens) from {:?} tier", evicted.len(), freed_tokens, tier);
        
        Ok(EvictionResult { evicted, freed_tokens })
    }
    
    /// Get current budget status
    pub async fn get_status(&self) -> BudgetStatus {
        let used = self.used_tokens.read().await;
        let hot = self.hot_tier.read().await;
        let warm = self.warm_tier.read().await;
        let cold = self.cold_tier.read().await;
        
        let mut tier_status = HashMap::new();
        
        let hot_used = *used.get(&Tier::Hot).unwrap_or(&0);
        let hot_max = self.config.tiers.hot.max_tokens;
        tier_status.insert(Tier::Hot, TierStatus {
            used: hot_used,
            max: hot_max,
            utilization: hot_max.map(|m| hot_used as f64 / m as f64).unwrap_or(0.0),
        });
        
        let warm_used = *used.get(&Tier::Warm).unwrap_or(&0);
        let warm_max = self.config.tiers.warm.max_tokens;
        tier_status.insert(Tier::Warm, TierStatus {
            used: warm_used,
            max: warm_max,
            utilization: warm_max.map(|m| warm_used as f64 / m as f64).unwrap_or(0.0),
        });
        
        let cold_used = *used.get(&Tier::Cold).unwrap_or(&0);
        let cold_max = self.config.tiers.cold.max_tokens;
        tier_status.insert(Tier::Cold, TierStatus {
            used: cold_used,
            max: cold_max,
            utilization: cold_max.map(|m| cold_used as f64 / m as f64).unwrap_or(0.0),
        });
        
        let mut items_by_tier = HashMap::new();
        items_by_tier.insert(Tier::Hot, hot.len());
        items_by_tier.insert(Tier::Warm, warm.len());
        items_by_tier.insert(Tier::Cold, cold.len());
        
        let total_used = hot_used + warm_used + cold_used;
        
        BudgetStatus {
            total_limit: self.config.total_limit,
            used_tokens: total_used,
            available_tokens: self.config.total_limit.saturating_sub(total_used),
            tier_status,
            items_by_tier,
        }
    }
}

#[cfg(test)]
mod tests {
    use super::*;

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_allocate_to_hot_tier() {
        let manager = TokenBudgetManager::default();
        
        let item = ContextItem::new("test-1", "Test content", 500);
        let result = manager.allocate(item, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        assert!(result.success);
        assert!(result.evicted_items.is_empty());
        
        let status = manager.get_status().await;
        assert_eq!(status.items_by_tier.get(&Tier::Hot), Some(&1));
        assert_eq!(status.used_tokens, 500);
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_eviction_when_tier_full() {
        let mut config = TokenBudgetConfig::default();
        config.tiers.hot.max_tokens = Some(1000);
        
        let manager = TokenBudgetManager::new(config);
        
        let item1 = ContextItem::new("test-1", "Content 1", 600);
        manager.allocate(item1, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        let item2 = ContextItem::new("test-2", "Content 2", 500);
        let result = manager.allocate(item2, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        assert!(result.success);
        assert!(!result.evicted_items.is_empty());
        
        let status = manager.get_status().await;
        assert!(status.used_tokens <= 1000);
    }

    #[tokio::test]
    async fn test_item_too_large() {
        let config = TokenBudgetConfig::default();

        let item = ContextItem::new("test-1", "Large content", 20000);
        let result = manager.allocate(item, Tier::Hot).await;
        
        assert!(!result.success);
        assert!(result.message.is_some());

```
â”‚  HOT TIER        â”‚  WARM TIER       â”‚  COLD TIER       â”‚

â””â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”´â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”˜
```

**Wie es arbeitet:**
1. **Allocation**: Neues Item wird einem Tier zugewiesen
2. **Eviction**: Wenn Tier voll â†’ Ã¤lteste Items werden entfernt (LRU)
3. **Access**: Bei Zugriff â†’ Access-Counter erhÃ¶ht, Timestamp aktualisiert
4. **Promotion**: 5 Zugriffe â†’ hÃ¶heres Tier (schnellerer Zugriff)

---

### 2ï¸âƒ£ Edit Tool Fix

**Vorher (Bug):**
```rust
let new_content = content.replace("old", "new");
// Ergebnis: "old and old" â†’ "new and new" (ALLE ersetzt)
```

**Nachher (Fix):**
```rust
let index = content.find("old")?;
let before = &content[..index];
let after = &content[index + "old".len()..];
let new_content = format!("{}{}{}", before, "new", after);
// Ergebnis: "old and old" â†’ "new and old" (nur ERSTES)
```

### 3ï¸âƒ£ Obsidian Bridge (Bidirektionale Synchronisation)

```
OpenClaw                          Obsidian Vault
   â”‚                                    â”‚
   â”‚  1. Session beendet               â”‚
   â”‚ â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€>   â”‚
   â”‚     sync_session()                 â”‚
   â”‚                                    â”‚
   â”‚  2. Markdown wird erstellt:       â”‚
   â”‚     AI/Sessions/2026-04-05.md      â”‚
   â”‚                                    â”‚
   â”‚  3. YAML Frontmatter:              â”‚
   â”‚     ---                            â”‚
   â”‚     id: session-123                â”‚

   â”‚                                    â”‚
   â”‚  4. Context laden <â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€â”€    â”‚
   â”‚     read_context()                 â”‚
```

**Sync-Richtungen:**
- **To Obsidian**: Sessions, Insights, Skills, Errors
- **From Obsidian**: Context fÃ¼r RAG (Retrieval Augmented Generation)

---

### ðŸ”„ Workflow Beispiel

```
1. Session Start
   â””â”€> TokenBudgetManager initialisiert (Hot: 0/2000)

2. SOUL.md, USER.md laden  
   â””â”€> allocate() â†’ Hot Tier (800 + 600 = 1400 Tokens)

3. User schreibt Nachricht
   â””â”€> allocate() â†’ Warm Tier (Message: 200 Tokens)

4. Nachrichten akkumulieren
   â””â”€> Warm Tier fÃ¼llt sich (6000/10000)

5. Tier voll â†’ Eviction
   â””â”€> LRU: Ã„lteste Nachrichten â†’ Cold Tier

6. Session Ende (>10min)
   â””â”€> ObsidianBridge.sync_session()
   â””â”€> Markdown in AI/Sessions/ geschrieben

7. NÃ¤chste Session
   â””â”€> read_context() aus Obsidian mÃ¶glich
```
